311.3(1): gsal/ cir yang sprul pa'i sku ni klong du bkra/ bon sku nam mkha' bzhin du mkha' 
311.4(1): mnyam yang / gzugs sku gzha' tshon bzhin du so sor gsal/ 'gro ba drang phyir 
311.5(1): gcig gis gcig bskyed nas/ gnas 'dir spyan 'dren char bzhin gshegs su 
311.6(1): gsol/ dmigs pa'i rten dang gdan la bzhugs su gsol/ mtshan brjod mi lang 
311.7(1): bder gshegs bsam mi khyab/ ci snyed sa yi rdul bas grangs mang ba'i/ 'gro ba'i

311.10(1): dbyings chen bon gyi dbyings dkyil te/ rang bzhin dkyil 'khor khyab gdal dam
